#a gift of onions
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2000
        desc = VIETmisc.2000.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
        is_triggered_only = yes
        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no
        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no        
        }
        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gregarious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = cruel
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = charitable
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = greedy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = just
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = wroth
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = proud
                }
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2000.a
                random_courtier = {
                        limit = {
                                is_female = no
                                NOT = {
                                        trait = incapable
                                }
                                war = no
                                prisoner = no
                                age = 16
                                in_command = no
                                is_abroad = no
                        }
                        reverse_opinion = {
                                modifier = opinion_happy
                                who = ROOT
                                years = 1
                        }
                }
                prestige = 1
        }
}

                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = proud
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = slothful
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = diligent
                }

                        factor = 2

                        factor = 0.5

                name = VIETmisc.2001.a

                        name = highly_amused_ruler

                }
        }
}

# cabbages are too lowly
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2002
        desc = VIETmisc.2002.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking
        is_triggered_only = yes
        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no
        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no        
                any_courtier = {
                            NOT = { trait = incapable }
                        war = no
                        prisoner = no
                        age = 16
                        in_command = no
                        is_abroad = no
                        OR = {
                                trait = proud
                                trait = gluttonous
                                trait = arbitrary
                        }
                }
        }
        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gregarious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = proud
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = ambitious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = content
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = paranoid
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = trusting
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = just
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = arbitrary
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = kind
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = cruel
                }
        }
        option = { # agree
                name = VIETmisc.2002.a
                random_list = {
                        70 = {}
                        30 = { add_trait = proud }
                }
                random_courtier = {
                        limit = {
                                NOT = {
                                        trait = incapable
                                }
                                war = no
                                prisoner = no
                                age = 16
                                in_command = no
                                is_abroad = no
                                OR = {
                                        trait = proud
                                        trait = gluttonous
                                        trait = arbitrary
                                }
                        }
                        opinion = {
                                modifier = opinion_satisfied
                                who = ROOT
                                years = 1
                        }
                }
        }
        option = { # disagree
                name = VIETmisc.2002.b
                random_list = {
                        70 = {}
                        30 = { add_trait = humble }
                }
                random_courtier = {
                        limit = {
                                NOT = {
                                        trait = incapable
                                }
                                war = no
                                prisoner = no
                                age = 16
                                in_command = no
                                is_abroad = no
                                OR = {
                                        trait = proud
                                        trait = gluttonous
                                        trait = arbitrary
                                }
                        }
                        opinion = {
                                modifier = opinion_disappointed
                                who = ROOT
                                years = 1
                        }
                }
        }
}

        }
}

# garlic vampires
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2004
        desc = VIETmisc.2004.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
        is_triggered_only = yes
        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no
        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no        
                OR = {
                        culture_group = central_germanic
                        culture_group = west_slavic
                        culture_group = south_slavic
                        culture_group = baltic
                        culture_group = east_slavic
                        culture = hungarian
                        culture = italian
                }
        }
        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = proud
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = paranoid
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = trusting
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = stressed
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = content
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = cynical
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = zealous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = depressed
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = patient
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = diligent
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = slothful
                }
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2004.a
                random_list = {
                        80 = {}
                        20 = { add_trait = paranoid }
                }                
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2004.b
                if = {
                        limit = {
                                NOT = { religion_group = pagan_group }
                        }
                        piety = 4
                }
                prestige = -5
                random_list = {
                        70 = {}
                        30 = { add_trait = cynical }
                }                
        }
}

# Greek salad
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2006
        desc = VIETmisc.2006.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest_greek
        is_triggered_only = yes
        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no
        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no        
                OR = {
                        culture = greek
                        culture = griko
                        capital_scope = {
                                OR = {
                                        culture = greek
                                        culture = griko
                                }
                        }
                }
        }
        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = proud
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = temperate
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = just
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = arbitrary
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = diligent
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = slothful
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = kind
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = cruel
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = patient
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = wroth
                }
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2005.a
                if = {
                        limit = {
                                trait = stressed
                        }
                        random_list = {
                                90 = {}
                                10 = { remove_trait = stressed }
                        }
                }
                if = {
                        limit = {
                                trait = depressed
                        }
                        random_list = {
                                90 = {}
                                10 = { remove_trait = depressed }
                        }
                }
                add_character_modifier = {
                        name = eating_good_food
                        duration = 180
                }
        }
}

character_event = {

        only_rulers = yes

			} 
		}
		any_realm_province = {
			OR = {
				culture = greek
				culture = griko
			} 
		}		
        }

        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gregarious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = temperate
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = proud
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = humble
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = wroth
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = patient

                modifier = {

        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2011.b

			75 = {}

		}          
        }
}

#what kinda coffee
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2012
        desc = VIETmisc.2012.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_feast
        is_triggered_only = yes

        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no

        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = east_african
			culture_group = arabic
			AND = {
				OR = {
					is_patrician = yes
					is_merchant_republic = yes
				}
				OR = {
					religion_group = muslim
					religion_group = zoroastrian_group
				}
			}
		}
		year = 1000        
        }

        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gregarious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = temperate
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = zealous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = arbitrary
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = diligent
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = slothful
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = ambitious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = hedonist
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.25
                        NOT = { year = 1285 }
                }
        }

        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2012.a
                piety = 1
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2012.b
                prestige = 1
        }
}

#bitter olives
character_event = {

        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1

        }
}

#the sexy arugula
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2014
        desc = VIETmisc.2014.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_maiden
        is_triggered_only = yes

        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no

        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no
		religion_group = christian        
        }

        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gregarious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = shy
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = temperate
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = lustful
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = chaste
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = arbitrary
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = zealous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = hedonist
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = celibate
                }
        }

               option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2014.a
		trigger = { NOT = { trait = celibate }}
                add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_feeling_sexy
			duration = 365
		}
		piety = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
			}
			random_list = {
				70 = { }
				30 = { add_trait = lustful }
			}
		}
        }
        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2014.b
		piety = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = chaste }
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = { }
				20 = { add_trait = chaste }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = { }
				20 = { add_trait = zealous }
			}
		}
	}
}

#popeye the sailor man
character_event = {
        id = VIETmisc.2015
        desc = VIETmisc.2015.desc
        picture = GFX_evt_vegetarian
        is_triggered_only = yes

        min_age = 16
        only_rulers = yes
        capable_only = yes
        prisoner = no

        trigger = {
                war = no
                in_command = no
                is_abroad = no        
        }

        weight_multiplier = {
                days = 1
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        is_patrician = yes
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = wroth
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = temperate
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = gluttonous
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = patient
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = slothful
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = ambitious
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        NOT = { martial = 7 }
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 2
                        trait = strong
                }
                modifier = {
                        factor = 0.5
                        trait = weak
                }
        }

        option = {
                name = VIETmisc.2015.a
		add_character_modifier = { 
			name = VIET_spinach_popeye 
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = popeye_spinach_eater }
	}
}

#quail egg cosmetics (I've eaten boiled quail eggs in Asian cuisine before, they can be tasty though they tend to be a bit harder than normal chicken eggs.)
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2016
	desc = VIETmisc.2016.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = israelite
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = north_african
			culture_group = latin
			culture_group = iberian
			culture_group = italian_group
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = fair
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ugly
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2016.a
		prestige = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2016.b
		random_list = {
			30 = { add_trait = gluttonous }
			70 = {}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2016.c
		piety = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2016.d
		trigger = { is_female = yes }
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_new_expensive_cosmetics
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

#egg shells
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2019
	desc = VIETmisc.2019.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no	
		any_vassal = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			ai = yes
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2019.a
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				ai = yes
			}
			prestige = -3
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_shamed_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.2019.b
		random_list = {
			75 = { }
			25 = { add_trait = content}
		}
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				ai = yes
			}
			prestige = -3
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_comforted_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
}




# deviled eggs
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2020
	desc = VIETmisc.2020.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_feast

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no	
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = { # stuffed with vegetables
		name = VIETmisc.2020.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
			}
			random_list = {
				30 = { add_trait = temperate }
				70 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = gluttonous
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { remove_trait = gluttonous }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 80
		}
	}

	option = { # stuffed with meat
		name = VIETmisc.2020.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 160
		}
	}


	option = { # stuffed with milk, cream, or cheese
		name = VIETmisc.2020.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = temperate }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { add_trait = gluttonous }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = temperate
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = { remove_trait = temperate }
				50 = {}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = eating_good_food
			duration = 320
		}
	}

}

# What to do with the unbeliever?
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2021
	desc = VIETmisc.2021.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_nightmare

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no
		religion = dulcinian
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = impaler
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			martial = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { martial = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = {#Kill Kill Kill
		name = VIETmisc.2021.a
		piety = 3
	}
	option = {#turn the other cheek
		name = VIETmisc.2021.b
		random_list = {
			50 = { piety = 5 }
			50 = { piety = -5 }			
		}
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			30 = { add_trait = kind }			
		}			
	}
	option = {#dont be a hypocrite
		name = VIETmisc.2021.c
		piety = -2
		prestige = 4
	}
}

# A bad bad vassal
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2023
	desc = VIETmisc.2023.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_emissary

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no
		religion = dulcinian
		any_vassal = {
			is_adult = yes
			is_feudal = yes
			religion = dulcinian
			wealth = 100
			ai = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = charitable }
			NOT = { trait = temperate }
			NOT = { trait = kind }
			NOT = { trait = just }			
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
	}

	option = {#give it back to the ppl
		name = VIETmisc.2023.a

character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2026
	desc = VIETmisc.2026.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_nightmare

	is_triggered_only = yes

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

	trigger = { 
		war = no 
		in_command = no 
		is_abroad = no
		culture = breton
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou }
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			trait = drunkard
		}
	}

	option = {#help him
		name = VIETmisc.2026.a
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
		add_trait = kind
		character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2027 tooltip = VIETmisc.2027.tooltip }
	}
	option = {#run away
		name = VIETmisc.2026.b
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = craven }
			10 = { add_trait = paranoid }			
		}			
	}
	option = {#ignore 
		name = VIETmisc.2026.c
		set_character_flag = VIET_met_ankou
	}
}

# Learning from the Wandering Hermit
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.10051
	desc = VIETmisc.10051.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_monastery_monks
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = yes
		war = no
		in_command = no
		learning = 9
		religion = fraticelli
		any_courtier = {
			trait = wandering_hermit
			religion = fraticelli
		}
		NOT ={ has_character_flag = VIET_fraticelli_preacher_learning }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = hedonist
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = charitable
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.10051.a"  #ok
		set_character_flag = VIET_fraticelli_preacher_learning
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				trait = wandering_hermit
				religion = fraticelli
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_shared_knowledge
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = { change_diplomacy = 1 }
			20 = { change_martial = 1 }
			20 = { change_stewardship = 1 }
			20 = { change_intrigue = 1 }
			20 = { change_learning = 1 }
		}
	}	
}

		modifier = {

			trait = charitable
		}

		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { year = 1350 }
		}
	}

		set_character_flag = VIET_has_hourglass
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_efficient_time
			duration = 1111
		}
	}

# Noontime hijinks
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2049
	desc = VIETmisc.2049.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_skyrim_forest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = yes
		war = no
		in_command = no
		month = 4
		NOT = { month = 9 }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}			
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = patient
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = proud
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gardener
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = scholar
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.2049.a"  #ok
		random = {
			chance = 5
			add_trait = ill
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = diligent
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				remove_trait = diligent
			}
		}
	}		
	option = {
		name = "VIETmisc.2049.b"  #ok
		tooltip_info = diligent
		trigger = {
			trait = diligent
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_trait = ill
		}
	}	
}

	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = content
			}
	}

	option = {#ignore it
		name = VIETmisc.2057.a
		prestige = 1
	}
	option = {#inspect it!
		name = VIETmisc.2057.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				NOT = { trait = charitable }
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { add_trait = greedy }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = greedy }
				trait = charitable
			}
			random_list = {
				75 = { }
				25 = { remove_trait = charitable }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_beggar_corpse_inspect }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2058 } }
				70 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2059 } }
				5 = { character_event = { id = VIETmisc.2060 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Shaft Head Tilts
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2098
	desc = VIETmisc.2098.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	min_age = 30
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_shaft_head_tilt }
		NOT = { trait = infirm }
		NOT = { trait = hunchback }
		OR = {
			diplomacy = 11
			intrigue = 11
		}
		diplomacy = 8
		intrigue = 8
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
			days = 1
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = gregarious
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = shy
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cruel
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = depressed
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = stressed
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cynical
			}
			modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					trait = zealous
			}
	}

			name = the_prude
			duration = 365
		}
	}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = scholar
		}
		modifier = {

		}

		name = VIETmisc.2101.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_loves_toothbrushing
			duration = -1
		}
		piety = 5
	}
	option = {#Nay
		name = VIETmisc.2101.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = zealous }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = { add_trait = cynical }
				60 = {}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = zealous
			}

				50 = { remove_trait = zealous }

			}
		}		
	}
}

			OR = {
				empire = { title = e_britannia }
				empire = { title = e_hre }
				empire = { title = e_carpathia }
				empire = { title = e_russia }
				empire = { title = e_france }
				empire = { title = e_scandinavia }
				empire = { title = e_wendish_empire }
				empire = { title = e_poland_lithuania }
				empire = { title = e_tartaria }
				terrain = steppe
				terrain = mountain
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2117.a
		random_lover = {
			opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_happy
					who = ROOT
					years = 1
			}	
			reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_happy
					who = ROOT
					years = 1
			}		
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_romantic_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Look up here
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2118
	desc = VIETmisc.2118.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_maiden

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_rulers = yes
	only_women = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		NOT = { trait = incapable }
		NOT = { trait = ugly }
		NOT = { trait = hunchback }
		NOT = { trait = imbecile }
		NOT = { trait = inbred }
		OR = {
			trait = fair
			trait = lustful
			trait = tall
			trait = fertile
			trait = gregarious
			trait = charismatic_negotiator
			trait = grey_eminence
			trait = strong
			trait = hedonist
			trait = proud
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			is_female = no
			NOT = { age = 28 }
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			OR = {
				trait = shy
				trait = kind
				trait = trusting
				trait = absentminded
				trait = patient
				trait = chaste
				NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
			}
			NOT = { trait = ugly }
			NOT = { trait = imbecile }
			NOT = { trait = inbred }
			NOT = { trait = lustful }
			NOT = { trait = cruel }
			NOT = { trait = lunatic }
			has_lover = no
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = fair
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			diplomacy = 13
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
	}

	option = {#angry!
		name = VIETmisc.2118.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				NOT = { age = 28 }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = kind
					trait = trusting
					trait = absentminded
					trait = patient
					trait = chaste
					NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
				}
				NOT = { trait = ugly }
				NOT = { trait = imbecile }
				NOT = { trait = inbred }
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				has_lover = no			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_eye_candy
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}	
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_angry
				who = ROOT
				years = 2
			}		
		}
	}
	option = {#seduce
		name = VIETmisc.2118.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 } 
		}
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				NOT = { age = 28 }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = kind
					trait = trusting
					trait = absentminded
					trait = patient
					trait = chaste
					NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
				}
				NOT = { trait = ugly }
				NOT = { trait = imbecile }
				NOT = { trait = inbred }
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				has_lover = no			
			}
			add_lover = ROOT	
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_cougar_har_har }
	}
	option = {#Ignore
		name = VIETmisc.2118.c
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				NOT = { age = 28 }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = kind
					trait = trusting
					trait = absentminded
					trait = patient
					trait = chaste
					NOT = { diplomacy = 7 }
				}
				NOT = { trait = ugly }
				NOT = { trait = imbecile }
				NOT = { trait = inbred }
				NOT = { trait = lustful }
				NOT = { trait = cruel }
				NOT = { trait = lunatic }
				has_lover = no			
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_eye_candy
				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			80 = {}
			20 = { add_trait = content }
		}
	}
	option = {#YES
		name = VIETmisc.2118.d
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				is_female = no
				NOT = { age = 28 }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				OR = {
					trait = shy
					trait = kind
					trait = trusting
					trait = absentminded
					trait = patient

				}

				NOT = { trait = cruel }

				has_lover = no			
			}
			opinion = {

				who = ROOT
				years = 3
			}	
		}
		random_list = {
			85 = {}

		}
	}

		}

			factor = 2

		}

			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = envious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
	}

	option = {#Yessiree

		}
	}
}

			factor = 0.5
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
	}

	option = {#Yessiree
		name = VIETmisc.2124.a
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_happy
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { age = 45 }
					is_female = yes
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					impregnate = ROOT
				}	
			}		
		}
	}
}

# Courtier of a different religion doesn't like sibling love
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2127
	desc = VIETmisc.2127.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = content }
			NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			NOT = { religion = messalian }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = proud
				trait = wroth
				trait = gregarious
				trait = envious
				trait = cruel
				trait = lustful
				trait = chaste
				trait = temperate
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
	}

	option = {#Buzz off
		name = VIETmisc.2127.a
		piety = 5
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = content }
				NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
				NOT = { religion = messalian }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = proud
					trait = wroth
					trait = gregarious
					trait = envious
					trait = cruel
					trait = lustful
					trait = chaste
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_disgusted
				who = ROOT
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#Silly
		name = VIETmisc.2127.b
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_religiously_tolerant_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
	}
}

# Exorcism with incest
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2128
	desc = VIETmisc.2128.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_holy_light_zoroastrian_group

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		religion_group = zoroastrian_group
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = VIET_incest_kills_demons }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { piety = 50 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			piety = 1000
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = deceitful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = honest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
	}

	option = {#hmm
		name = VIETmisc.2128.a
		piety = 5
		set_character_flag = VIET_incest_kills_demons
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_incest_demon_exorcist
			duration = 1453
		}
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			piety = 5
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_incest_demon_exorcist
				duration = 1453
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#hmm
		name = VIETmisc.2128.b
		trigger = { #See? I think of everything
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_koyomi
					is_female = no
					any_spouse = {
						sibling = ROOT
						religion = ROOT
						has_character_flag = VIET_karen
						is_female = yes
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_character_flag = VIET_karen
					is_female = yes
					any_spouse = {
						sibling = ROOT
						religion = ROOT
						has_character_flag = VIET_koyomi
						is_female = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
			piety = 5
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_incest_demon_exorcist
				duration = 1453
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = VIET_incest_kills_demons
	}
}

# Someone don't like hummus
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2151
	desc = VIETmisc.2151.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_scandal

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = north_african
			culture_group = israelite
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		any_vassal = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_hummus_hater }
			ai = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			any_vassal = {
				has_character_modifier = VIET_hummus_hater
			}
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = proud
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = humble
		}
	}

	option = {#not ok
		name = VIETmisc.2151.a
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_hummus_hater }
				ai = yes
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_hummus_hater
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fine hummus region rising
province_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2152
	desc = VIETmisc.2152.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hummus
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			culture_group = arabic
			culture_group = north_african
			culture_group = israelite
			culture_group = iranian
			culture_group = byzantine
			culture = turkish
		}
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region }
		NOT = { has_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter }
		NOT = {
			kingdom = { 
				any_realm_province = {
					has_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3456
	}

	option = {#not ok
		name = VIETmisc.2152.a
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = VIET_hummus_producing_region
			duration = -1
		}
		set_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter
	}
}

	}

		name = VIETmisc.2153.a
		remove_province_modifier = VIET_hummus_producing_region
		clr_province_flag = VIET_hummus_producing_region_counter
	}
}

# Critical infidels
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2161
	desc = VIETmisc.2161.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_heretic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
			NOT = { religion = messalian }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist }
			#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			diplomacy = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = patient
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = zealous
		}
	}

	option = {#u will luv Ncest or else
		name = VIETmisc.2161.a
		piety = 15
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = zoroastrian_group }
				NOT = { religion = messalian }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist }
				#NOT = { religion = zunist_reformed }			
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = VIET_enforcing_incest
				duration = 800
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#go 2 hell
		name = VIETmisc.2161.b
		piety = -10
		random_list = {
			70 = { }
			20 = { add_trait = content }
			10 = { add_trait = slothful }
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = VIET_no_incest_hell }
	}

	option = {#respect, bro
		name = VIETmisc.2161.c
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = VIET_religiously_tolerant_ruler
			duration = 1227
		}
	}
}

	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes

			#religion = zunist

		}
		any_spouse = {
			sibling = ROOT
			religion = ROOT
			opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
		}
		NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 }
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = brave
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = craven
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
	}

	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2170.a
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
		piety = 5
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }			
			}
			piety = 5
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { num_of_lovers = 5 }
					NOT = { is_lover = ROOT }
				}
				random = {
					add_lover = ROOT
					chance = 25
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#world peace thru incest
		name = VIETmisc.2170.b
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
		piety = 5
		random_spouse = {
			limit = {
				sibling = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }			
			}
			piety = 5
			if = {

		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { age = 35 }

			opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_adult = yes
			age = 35

		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = kind
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cruel
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

		}

# Courtier obsessed with incest
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.2188
	desc = VIETmisc.2188.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_courtiers_talking

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	min_age = 16
	only_rulers = yes
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		war = no
		in_command = no
		is_abroad = no
		OR = {
			religion_group = zoroastrian_group
			religion = messalian
			#religion = zunist
			#religion = zunist_reformed
		}
		NOT = {
			any_courtier = {
				has_character_modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_incest			
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			is_female = no
			is_adult = yes
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = cynical }
			NOT = { trait = imbecile }
			NOT = { trait = slow }
			religion = ROOT
			diplomacy = 8
			OR = {
				trait = zealous
				trait = scholar
				trait = quick
				trait = genius
				trait = charismatic_negotiator
				trait = grey_eminence
				learning = 14
				AND = {
					trait = lustful
					diplomacy = 11
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = VIET_obsessed_with_incest }
		}
	}
	
	weight_multiplier = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = shy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			learning = 12
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { learning = 8 }
		}
	}

	option = {#creepy
		name = VIETmisc.2188.a
		random_courtier = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = cynical }
				NOT = { trait = imbecile }
				NOT = { trait = slow }
				religion = ROOT
				diplomacy = 8
				OR = {
					trait = zealous
					trait = scholar
					trait = quick
					trait = genius
					trait = charismatic_negotiator
					trait = grey_eminence
					learning = 14
					AND = {
						trait = lustful
						diplomacy = 11
					}
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = VIET_obsessed_with_incest
				duration = 5555
			}

		}
	}

			name = VIET_annoyed_ruler
			duration = 365
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			character_event = { id = VIETceltic.2217 }
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = greedy
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = just
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = arbitrary
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = diligent  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = trusting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = paranoid
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = gluttonous  
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
	}

	option = {#ok
		name = VIETmisc.2222.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = best_meal_in_ages
			duration = 468
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trait = gluttonous
					trait = gregarious
					trait = trusting
				}
			}
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = best_meal_in_ages
				duration = 468
			}
		}
	}
}

#Blind character's other senses improve
character_event = {
	id = VIETmisc.3000
	desc = VIETmisc.3000.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers

	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			trait = blinded
			trait = born_blind
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2000
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = absentminded
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = perceptive
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = genius
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			trait = slow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			trait = quick
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = VIETmisc.3000.a
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = blind_increased_senses
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
